           <div class="panel-content"> 
            <h3 class="c-heading-5">Bring out your best</h3> 
            <div class="c-paragraph-2">
             <p>Write and present like a pro with editing and writing options in Word and layout suggestions and coaching in PowerPoint. Youll have access to smart assistance features and premium creative content in each app. Choose from thousands of curated stock images, icons, and fonts to add your own flair quickly and beautifully.</p>

           <div class="panel-content"> 
            <h3 class="c-heading-5">Protect whats important</h3> 
            <div class="c-paragraph-2">
             <p>Back up and access photos and files with 1 TB of OneDrive cloud storage. Plus, with your own Personal Vault folder you get an added layer of security with two-step identity verification for your most important files. OneDrive also has built-in ransomware detection and recovery capability, so everything you save is protected against digital attacks.<sup>2</sup></p> 
            </div> 
           </div> 
          </div>

            <div class="c-paragraph-2">
             <p>Whether its a school assignment, newsletter, or virtual get-together, you can seamlessly meet up and work with others at the same time to complete projects faster and stay connected. Its easy to share OneDrive files from your PC or mobile device and let friends, classmates, or family view, make suggestions and edit the document.</p>

       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div id="coreui-space-h6ejart" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;Space 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-Space&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m11r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:11,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r4a2&quot;}" data-module-id="PDP-RT-Office-Template|OverviewTab|coreui-region|coreui-space-h6ejart|coreui-space"> 
       <div class="m-small-space"> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-9t5q583" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;CollapsibleDrawer 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-collapsibledrawer&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m12r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:12,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r4a2&quot;}" data-module-id="PDP-RT-Office-Template|OverviewTab|coreui-region|coreui-collapsibledrawer-9t5q583|coreui-collapsibledrawer"> 
       <section class="cui-drawer"> 
        <div class="cui-header f-divider"> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn1m12r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m12r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-9t5q583-collapsible-drawer0">What is the difference between Office 2019 (one-time purchase) and Microsoft 365 (subscription)?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-9t5q583-collapsible-drawer0" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>Office 2019 is sold as a one-time purchase, which means you pay a single, up-front cost to get Office apps for one computer. One-time purchases are available for both PCs and Macs. However, there are no upgrade options which means if you plan to upgrade to the next major release, you'll have to buy it at full price.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>Microsoft 365 is a subscription that includes the most collaborative, up-to-date features in one seamless, integrated experience. Microsoft 365 includes the robust Office desktop apps that youre familiar with, like Word, PowerPoint, and Excel. You also get extra online storage and cloud-connected features that let you collaborate on files in real time. With a subscription, you'll always have the latest features, fixes, and security updates along with ongoing tech support at no extra cost. You can choose to pay for your subscription on a monthly or yearly basis, and the Microsoft 365 Family plan lets you share your subscription with your family for up to 6 people, and use your apps on multiple PCs, Macs, tablets, and phones.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn2m12r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:2,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m12r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-9t5q583-collapsible-drawer1">I'm an existing O365 subscriber. What does this mean for me?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-9t5q583-collapsible-drawer1" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>This means that your Office 365 subscription will automatically be renamed to Microsoft 365.&nbsp;Get everything you love about Office 365, plus the additional benefits as they are released, all at the same price. No action is needed from your end.&nbsp;Changes will begin starting April 21, 2020.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn3m12r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:3,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m12r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-9t5q583-collapsible-drawer2">How do I know if my PC or Mac can run Microsoft 365?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-9t5q583-collapsible-drawer2" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>Microsoft 365 is compatible with PC, Mac, Android, and iOS. See <a href="https://office.com/systemrequirements" class="c-hyperlink">system requirements</a> for compatible versions of your devices, and for other feature requirements.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn4m12r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:4,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m12r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-9t5q583-collapsible-drawer3">Will Microsoft 365 be identical on a PC and on a Mac?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-9t5q583-collapsible-drawer3" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>No. Microsoft 365s applications are tailored for each platform and each operating system. The applications available for Mac users and the specific features included may be different from those available for PC users. With Microsoft 365, you can be flexible. With your account, you are not limited to exclusively Mac or exclusively PC, so you can transition across devices.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn5m12r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:5,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m12r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-9t5q583-collapsible-drawer4">Do I keep control of my documents with a Microsoft 365 subscription?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-9t5q583-collapsible-drawer4" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>Yes. Documents that you have created belong fully to you. You can choose to store them online on OneDrive or locally on your PC or Mac.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn6m12r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:6,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m12r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-9t5q583-collapsible-drawer5">Is internet access required for Microsoft 365?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-9t5q583-collapsible-drawer5" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>Internet access is required to install and activate all the latest releases of apps and services included in all Microsoft 365 subscription plans. Note that if you are an existing subscriber, you do not need to reinstall or purchase another subscription.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>For Microsoft 365 plans, Internet access is also needed to manage your subscription account, for example to install Office apps on other PCs or to change billing options. Internet access is also required to access documents stored on OneDrive, unless you install the <a href="https://products.office.com/microsoft-office-for-home-and-school-faq#cd6f27d6-3bb0-22a8-9228-1385af8f3445" class="c-hyperlink">OneDrive desktop app</a>.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>You should also connect to the Internet regularly to keep your version of Microsoft 365 up to date and to benefit from automatic upgrades. If you do not connect to the Internet at least every 31 days, your apps will go into reduced functionality mode, which means that you can view or print your documents but cannot edit the documents or create new ones. To reactivate your apps, simply reconnect to the Internet.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>You do not need to be connected to the Internet to use the Office apps, such as Word, Excel, and PowerPoint, because the apps are fully installed on your computer.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn7m12r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:7,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m12r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-9t5q583-collapsible-drawer6">What is a Microsoft account and why do I need it for Microsoft 365?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-9t5q583-collapsible-drawer6" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>Your Microsoft account is the combination of an email address and password that you use to sign in to services like OneDrive, Xbox LIVE, and Outlook.com. If you use any of these services, you already have a Microsoft account that you can use or you can create a new account. <a href="http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=403717" class="c-hyperlink">Learn more about a Microsoft account</a>.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>As part of signing up for a trial or purchasing Microsoft 365, you will be prompted to sign in with a Microsoft account. You must be signed in with this account to install and manage your Microsoft 365 subscription, or to use some subscription benefits, including OneDrive storage.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn8m12r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:8,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m12r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-9t5q583-collapsible-drawer7">How many people can use a Microsoft 365 subscription?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-9t5q583-collapsible-drawer7" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>You can share Microsoft 365 Family with 5 other people in your household, for a total of 6 users. Microsoft 365 Personal can be used by one person.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn9m12r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:9,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m12r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-9t5q583-collapsible-drawer8">How do I share my subscription benefits with members of my family?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-9t5q583-collapsible-drawer8" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>If you have an active Microsoft 365 Family subscription, you can share it with up to five members of your household. Each household member you share your subscription with can install Microsoft 365 on all their devices and sign in to five devices at the same time.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>To add someone to your subscription, visit <a href="https://account.microsoft.com" class="c-hyperlink">https://account.microsoft.com</a> and follow the on-screen instructions to add a user. Each person you add will receive an email with the steps they need to follow. Once they have accepted and completed the steps, their information, including the installs they are using, will appear on their My Account page. You can stop sharing your subscription with someone or remove a device they are using at <a href="https://account.microsoft.com" class="c-hyperlink">https://account.microsoft.com</a>.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn10m12r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:10,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m12r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-9t5q583-collapsible-drawer9">If Im not paying for a subscription, what do I get for free?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-9t5q583-collapsible-drawer9" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>Visit <a href="https://products.office.com/free-productivity-apps" class="c-hyperlink">this page</a> to learn more about free apps.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </section>

    <section id="pivot-RequirementsTab" role="tabpanel" aria-label="requirements" aria-hidden="true"> 
     <div id="RequirementsTab" role="region" class="f-center f-active-bold" data-region-key="requirementstab" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;RequirementsTab 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Region_coreui-region&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;r5a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:5,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;a2&quot;}"> 
      <div id="coreui-contenthighlight-gcuahm0" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;R1ContentHighlight 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-contenthighlight&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m1r5a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r5a2&quot;}" data-module-id="PDP-RT-Office-Template|RequirementsTab|coreui-region|coreui-contenthighlight-gcuahm0|coreui-contenthighlight"> 
       <div role="presentation" class="m-heading-4"> 
        <h2 class="c-heading">Requirements</h2> 
       </div> 
       <div class="m-content-placement x-clearfix content-highlight"> 
        <div data-grid="col-12 stack-3"> 
         <div data-grid="col-6 pad-6x"> 
          <div data-grid="col-6"> 
           <div class="m-content-placement-item f-size-medium"> 
            <h3 class="c-heading">PC</h3> 
            <div class="c-paragraph">
             <p><strong>Computer and processor</strong><br> 1.6 gigahertz (GHz) or faster, 2-core</p> 
             <p>&nbsp;</p> 
             <p><strong>Operating System</strong><br> Windows 10, Windows 8.1<br> &nbsp;</p> 
             <p>For the best experience, use the latest version of any operating system specified above</p> 
             <p>&nbsp;</p> 
             <p>&nbsp;</p> 
             <p><strong>Memory</strong><br> 4GB RAM<br> 2 GB RAM (32-bit)</p> 
             <p>&nbsp;</p> 
             <p><strong>Hard Disk</strong><br> 4.0 GB of available disk space</p> 
             <p>&nbsp;</p> 
             <p>&nbsp;</p> 
             <p>&nbsp;</p> 
             <p><strong>Display</strong><br> 1280 x 768 screen resolution</p> 
             <p>&nbsp;</p> 
             <p><strong>Graphics</strong><br> Graphics hardware acceleration requires DirectX 9 or later, with WDDM 2.0 or higher for Windows 10 (or WDDM 1.3 or higher for Windows 10 Fall Creators Update).</p> 
             <p>&nbsp;</p> 
             <p><strong>.NET version</strong><br> Some features may require .NET 3.5 or 4.6 and higher to also be installed</p> 
            </div> 
           </div> 
          </div> 
          <div data-grid="col-6"> 
           <div class="m-content-placement-item f-size-medium"> 
            <h3 class="c-heading">Mac</h3> 
            <div class="c-paragraph">
             <p><strong>Computer and processor</strong><br> Intel processor</p> 
             <p>&nbsp;</p> 
             <p><strong>Operating System</strong><br> The three most recent versions of macOS</p> 
             <p>&nbsp;</p> 
             <p>For the best experience, use the latest versions of any operating system specified above.&nbsp;</p> 
             <p>&nbsp;</p> 
             <p><strong>Memory</strong><br> 4 GB RAM</p> 
             <p>&nbsp;</p> 
             <p>&nbsp;</p> 
             <p><strong>Hard Disk</strong><br> 10 GB of available disk space. HFS+ hard disk format (also known as Mac OS Extended or APFS)</p> 
             <p>&nbsp;</p> 
             <p><strong>Display</strong><br> 1280 x 800 screen resolution</p> 
             <p>&nbsp;</p> 
             <p><strong>Graphics</strong><br> No graphics requirements</p> 
            </div> 
           </div> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <div data-grid="col-6 pad-6x"> 
          <div data-grid="col-6"> 
           <div class="m-content-placement-item f-size-medium"> 
            <h3 class="c-heading">Android</h3> 
            <div class="c-paragraph">
             <p><strong>Computer and processor</strong><br> ARM-based or Intel x86 processor</p> 
             <p>&nbsp;</p> 
             <p><strong>Operating System</strong><br> The last 4 major versions of Android<br> &nbsp;</p> 
             <p>For the best experience, use the latest version of any operating system specified above</p> 
             <p>&nbsp;</p> 
             <p>&nbsp;</p> 
             <p><strong>Memory</strong><br> 1GB</p> 
            </div> 
           </div> 
          </div> 
          <div data-grid="col-6"> 
           <div class="m-content-placement-item f-size-medium"> 
            <h3 class="c-heading">iOS</h3> 
            <div class="c-paragraph">
             <p><strong>Computer and processor</strong><br> N/A</p> 
             <p>&nbsp;</p> 
             <p><strong>Operating System</strong><br> The two most recent versions of iOS&nbsp;<br> &nbsp;</p> 
             <p>For the best experience, use the latest version of any operating system specified above</p> 
            </div> 
           </div> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div id="coreui-contentrichblock-xt5zdno" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;RichText 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-contentrichblock&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m2r5a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:2,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r5a2&quot;}" data-module-id="PDP-RT-Office-Template|RequirementsTab|coreui-region|coreui-contentrichblock-xt5zdno|coreui-contentrichblock"> 
       <div data-grid="col-12" class="m-rich-content-block context-ucx"> 
        <p><strong>Browser</strong><br> The current version of Microsoft Edge, Internet Explorer, Safari, Chrome, or Firefox.&nbsp;<a class="c-hyperlink" href="https://products.office.com/office-resources#coreui-heading-uyetipy">Get more details</a>.</p> 
        <p><strong>Other</strong><br> Internet functionality requires an Internet connection. Fees may apply.<br> A touch-enabled device is required to use any multi-touch functionality. But, all features and functionality are always available by using a keyboard, mouse, or other standard or accessible input device.<br> Product functionality and graphics may vary based on your system configuration. Some features may require additional or advanced hardware or server connectivity.</p>

    <section id="pivot-FAQTab" role="tabpanel" aria-label="faq" aria-hidden="true"> 
     <div id="FAQTab" role="region" class="f-center f-active-bold" data-region-key="faqtab" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;FAQTab 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Region_coreui-region&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:6,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;a2&quot;}"> 
      <div id="coreui-contentrichblock-i6o7mvc" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;RichText 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-contentrichblock&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m1r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r6a2&quot;}" data-module-id="PDP-RT-Office-Template|FAQTab|coreui-region|coreui-contentrichblock-i6o7mvc|coreui-contentrichblock"> 
       <div data-grid="col-12" class="m-rich-content-block context-ucx"> 
        <p><strong>Frequently asked questions</strong></p> 
        <p>Find answers to commonly asked questions about Microsoft&nbsp;365.</p> 
        <p><a href="#coreui-areaheading-ap15bbe" class="c-hyperlink">Top questions</a><br> <a href="#coreui-areaheading-qk8hunr" class="c-hyperlink">Existing Subscribers</a><br> <a href="#coreui-areaheading-rvk7zwi" class="c-hyperlink">Language availability for Microsoft 365</a><br> <a href="#coreui-areaheading-oogixx9" class="c-hyperlink">Managing your Microsoft 365 subscription</a><br> <a href="#coreui-areaheading-nf1fizl" class="c-hyperlink">Renewals, cancellations, and billing</a></p> 
       </div>

      <div id="coreui-areaheading-ap15bbe" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;AreaHeading 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-areaheading&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m2r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:2,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r6a2&quot;}" data-module-id="PDP-RT-Office-Template|FAQTab|coreui-region|coreui-areaheading-ap15bbe|coreui-areaheading"> 
       <div class="m-area-heading"> 
        <h2 class="c-heading">Top Questions</h2> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div id="coreui-space-tf0nbcq" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;Space 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-Space&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m3r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:3,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r6a2&quot;}" data-module-id="PDP-RT-Office-Template|FAQTab|coreui-region|coreui-space-tf0nbcq|coreui-space"> 
       <div class="m-small-space"> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-1ywrjve" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;CollapsibleDrawer 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-collapsibledrawer&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m4r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:4,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r6a2&quot;}" data-module-id="PDP-RT-Office-Template|FAQTab|coreui-region|coreui-collapsibledrawer-1ywrjve|coreui-collapsibledrawer"> 
       <section class="cui-drawer"> 
        <div class="cui-header f-divider"> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn1m4r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m4r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-1ywrjve-collapsible-drawer0">What is the difference between Office 2019 (one-time purchase) and Microsoft 365 (subscription)?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-1ywrjve-collapsible-drawer0" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>Office 2019 is sold as a <i>one-time purchase</i>, which means you pay a single, up-front cost to get Office apps for one computer. One-time purchases are available for both PCs and Macs. However, there are no upgrade options which means if you plan to upgrade to the next major release, you'll have to buy it at full price.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>Microsoft 365 is a subscription that includes the most collaborative, up-to-date features in one seamless, integrated experience. Microsoft 365 includes the robust Office desktop apps that youre familiar with, like Word, PowerPoint, and Excel. You also get extra online storage and cloud-connected features that let you collaborate on files in real time. With a subscription, you'll always have the latest features, fixes, and security updates along with ongoing tech support at no extra cost. You can choose to pay for your subscription on a monthly or yearly basis, and the Microsoft 365 Family plan lets you share your subscription with your family for up to 6 people, and use your apps on multiple PCs, Macs, tablets, and phones.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn2m4r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:2,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m4r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-1ywrjve-collapsible-drawer1">I'm an existing O365 subscriber. What does this mean for me?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-1ywrjve-collapsible-drawer1" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>This means that your Office 365 subscription will automatically be renamed to Microsoft 365.&nbsp;Get everything you love about Office 365, plus the additional benefits as they are released, all at the same price. No action is needed from your end.&nbsp;Changes will begin starting April 21, 2020.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn3m4r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:3,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m4r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-1ywrjve-collapsible-drawer2">How do I know if my PC or Mac can run Microsoft 365?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-1ywrjve-collapsible-drawer2" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>Microsoft 365 is compatible with PC, Mac, Android, and iOS. See <a href="https://office.com/systemrequirements" class="c-hyperlink">system requirements</a> for compatible versions of your devices, and for other feature requirements.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn4m4r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:4,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m4r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-1ywrjve-collapsible-drawer3">Will Microsoft 365 be identical on a PC and on a Mac?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-1ywrjve-collapsible-drawer3" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>No. Microsoft 365s applications are tailored for each platform and each operating system. The applications available for Mac users and the specific features included may be different from those available for PC users. With Microsoft 365, you can be flexible. With your account, you are not limited to exclusively Mac or exclusively PC, so you can transition across devices.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn5m4r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:5,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m4r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-1ywrjve-collapsible-drawer4">Do I keep control of my documents with a Microsoft 365 subscription?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-1ywrjve-collapsible-drawer4" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>Yes. Documents that you have created belong fully to you. You can choose to store them online on OneDrive or locally on your PC or Mac.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn6m4r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:6,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m4r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-1ywrjve-collapsible-drawer5">Is internet access required for Microsoft 365?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-1ywrjve-collapsible-drawer5" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>Internet access is required to install and activate all the latest releases of apps and services included in all Microsoft 365 subscription plans. Note that if you are an existing subscriber, you do not need to reinstall or purchase another subscription.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>For Microsoft 365 plans, Internet access is also needed to manage your subscription account, for example to install Office apps on other PCs or to change billing options. Internet access is also required to access documents stored on OneDrive, unless you install the <a class="c-hyperlink" href="https://products.office.com/microsoft-office-for-home-and-school-faq#cd6f27d6-3bb0-22a8-9228-1385af8f3445">OneDrive desktop app</a>.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>You should also connect to the Internet regularly to keep your version of Microsoft 365 up to date and to benefit from automatic upgrades. If you do not connect to the Internet at least every 31 days, your apps will go into reduced functionality mode, which means that you can view or print your documents but cannot edit the documents or create new ones. To reactivate your apps, simply reconnect to the Internet.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>You do not need to be connected to the Internet to use the Office apps, such as Word, Excel, and PowerPoint, because the apps are fully installed on your computer.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn7m4r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:7,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m4r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-1ywrjve-collapsible-drawer6">What is a Microsoft account and why do I need it for Microsoft 365?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-1ywrjve-collapsible-drawer6" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>Your Microsoft account is the combination of an email address and password that you use to sign in to services like OneDrive, Xbox LIVE, and Outlook.com. If you use any of these services, you already have a Microsoft account that you can use or you can create a new account. <a class="c-hyperlink" href="http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=403717">Learn more about a Microsoft account</a>.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>As part of signing up for a trial or purchasing Microsoft 365, you will be prompted to sign in with a Microsoft account. You must be signed in with this account to install and manage your Microsoft 365 subscription, or to use some subscription benefits, including OneDrive storage.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn8m4r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:8,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m4r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-1ywrjve-collapsible-drawer7">How many people can use a Microsoft 365 subscription?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-1ywrjve-collapsible-drawer7" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>You can share Microsoft 365 Family with 5 other people in your household, for a total of 6 users. Microsoft 365 Personal can be used by one person.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn9m4r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:9,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m4r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-1ywrjve-collapsible-drawer8">How do I share my subscription benefits with members of my family?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-1ywrjve-collapsible-drawer8" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>If you have an active Microsoft 365 Family subscription, you can share it with up to five members of your household. Each household member you share your subscription with can install Microsoft 365 on all their devices and sign in to five devices at the same time.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>To add someone to your subscription, visit <a class="c-hyperlink" href="https://account.microsoft.com/">https://account.microsoft.com</a> and follow the on-screen instructions to add a user. Each person you add will receive an email with the steps they need to follow. Once they have accepted and completed the steps, their information, including the installs they are using, will appear on their My Account page. You can stop sharing your subscription with someone or remove a device they are using at <a class="c-hyperlink" href="https://account.microsoft.com/">https://account.microsoft.com</a>.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn10m4r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:10,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m4r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-1ywrjve-collapsible-drawer9">If Im not paying for a subscription, what do I get for free?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-1ywrjve-collapsible-drawer9" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>Visit <a href="https://products.office.com/free-productivity-apps" class="c-hyperlink">this page</a> to learn more about free apps.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </section>

       <div class="m-area-heading"> 
        <h2 class="c-heading">Existing Subscribers</h2> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div id="coreui-space-vld3jeh" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;Space 2&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-Space&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m6r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:6,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r6a2&quot;}" data-module-id="PDP-RT-Office-Template|FAQTab|coreui-region|coreui-space-vld3jeh|coreui-space"> 
       <div class="m-small-space"> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;CollapsibleDrawer 2&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-collapsibledrawer&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m7r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:7,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r6a2&quot;}" data-module-id="PDP-RT-Office-Template|FAQTab|coreui-region|coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq|coreui-collapsibledrawer"> 
       <section class="cui-drawer"> 
        <div class="cui-header f-divider"> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn1m7r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m7r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer0">Im an existing Office 365 subscriber. What does this mean for me?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer0" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>This means that your Office 365 subscription will automatically be renamed to Microsoft 365. No action is needed from your end.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn2m7r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:2,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m7r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer1">Will I have to pay more?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer1" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>No, your subscription cost will not change.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn3m7r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:3,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m7r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer2">When will the change occur?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer2" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>Changes begin starting April 21, 2020.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn4m7r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:4,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m7r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer3">Which version of Microsoft 365 will I receive?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer3" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>If you are an Office 365 Personal subscriber, you will be switched to a Microsoft 365 Personal subscription.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>If you are an Office 365 Home subscriber, you will be switched to a Microsoft 365 Family subscription.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>If you are an Office 365 Solo subscriber (available only in Japan), you will be switched to a Microsoft 365 Personal subscription.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn5m7r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:5,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m7r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer4">Where and how do I access my new features for Microsoft 365?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer4" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>You can access new features through your <a href="https://account.microsoft.com/" class="c-hyperlink">Microsoft account portal</a>. <a href="http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=403717" class="c-hyperlink">Learn more about a Microsoft account</a>.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn6m7r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:6,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m7r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer5">What do I need to do to start using Microsoft 365?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer5" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>You do not need to take any additional action to start using Microsoft 365 as your existing Office 365 subscription will transition automatically to Microsoft 365.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn7m7r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:7,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m7r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer6">Will I be able to open my Office 365 files in Microsoft 365?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer6" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>Yes, you will be able to open Office 365 files in Microsoft 365.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn8m7r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:8,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m7r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer7">I already bought a pre-paid subscription for Office 365. What happens now?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer7" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>The subscription will be automatically converted to Microsoft 365 at redemption. The user will receive a transition message communicating that Office 365 is now Microsoft 365.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn9m7r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:9,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m7r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer8">What is the difference between Office 365 and Microsoft 365?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer8" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>Microsoft 365 includes everything you love about Office 365 and more, at the same price. Weve added value to the Office 365 subscription to make it Microsoft 365. With Microsoft 365, you receive additional benefits including Microsoft Editor, Money in Excel, and premium creative content in Office, plus more to come.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn10m7r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:10,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m7r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer9">Why did you change the name from Office 365 to Microsoft 365?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer9" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>We changed the name to be more reflective of the range of benefits within the subscription, which now extend beyond premium Office apps to include more value.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn11m7r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:11,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m7r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer10">Does the change from Office 365 to Microsoft 365 affect how I share my Microsoft 365 Family subscription with others?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer10" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>You will still have the same users on your new Microsoft 365 Family subscription - up to five other family members within your home, (unrelated) roommates, or even remote family members.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn12m7r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:12,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m7r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer11">When&nbsp;I share my subscription with others will they also be able to see one anothers OneDrive files?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-w0c8lyq-collapsible-drawer11" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>The files and folders you store in OneDrive are private. If youd like, you can use OneDrive to share photos, Microsoft Office documents, other files, and entire folders with people. You can <a href="https://support.office.com/article/see-who-a-file-is-shared-with-in-onedrive-or-sharepoint-51bb79a9-b696-410d-a7a7-c320e541272d" class="c-hyperlink">see who a OneDrive file is shared with</a> or <a href="https://support.office.com/article/stop-sharing-onedrive-or-sharepoint-files-or-folders-or-change-permissions-0a36470f-d7fe-40a0-bd74-0ac6c1e13323" class="c-hyperlink">stop sharing</a> at any time.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div>

      </div> 
      <div id="coreui-areaheading-rvk7zwi" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;AreaHeading 3&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-areaheading&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m8r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:8,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r6a2&quot;}" data-module-id="PDP-RT-Office-Template|FAQTab|coreui-region|coreui-areaheading-rvk7zwi|coreui-areaheading"> 
       <div class="m-area-heading"> 
        <h2 class="c-heading">Language availability for Microsoft 365</h2> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div id="coreui-space-qpgcfhp" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;Space 3&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-Space&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m9r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:9,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r6a2&quot;}" data-module-id="PDP-RT-Office-Template|FAQTab|coreui-region|coreui-space-qpgcfhp|coreui-space"> 
       <div class="m-small-space"> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-defpx5e" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;CollapsibleDrawer 3&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-collapsibledrawer&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m10r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:10,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r6a2&quot;}" data-module-id="PDP-RT-Office-Template|FAQTab|coreui-region|coreui-collapsibledrawer-defpx5e|coreui-collapsibledrawer"> 
       <section class="cui-drawer"> 
        <div class="cui-header f-divider"> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn1m10r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m10r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-defpx5e-collapsible-drawer0">For which languages is Microsoft 365 available?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-defpx5e-collapsible-drawer0" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>Microsoft 365 plans are available in <a href="https://products.office.com/choose-valid-billing-market" class="c-hyperlink">most countries/regions</a>. In countries/regions where Microsoft 365 plans are not available, you can still buy an Office 2019 suite, a one-time purchase which includes 2019 versions of the Office apps, but no additional security or storage features. When buying Microsoft 365, its important that you select the country/region in which you will be billed and in which youll use the software. Selecting a different country/region may cause problems with subscription setup and renewal.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn2m10r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:2,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m10r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-defpx5e-collapsible-drawer1">Can I use Microsoft 365 in languages other than the one I originally purchased?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-defpx5e-collapsible-drawer1" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>Yes. Microsoft offers simple and cost-effective solutions for multilingual individuals, families, and small businesses. Each time you install Office apps on an additional PC or Mac at, you <a href="https://account.microsoft.com/services/office/overview" class="c-hyperlink">can choose the language in which to install</a>.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </section> 
      </div> 
      <div id="coreui-areaheading-oogixx9" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;AreaHeading 4&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-areaheading&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m11r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:11,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r6a2&quot;}" data-module-id="PDP-RT-Office-Template|FAQTab|coreui-region|coreui-areaheading-oogixx9|coreui-areaheading"> 
       <div class="m-area-heading"> 
        <h2 class="c-heading">Managing your Microsoft 365 subscription</h2> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div id="coreui-space-48pxaqz" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;Space 4&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-Space&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m12r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:12,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r6a2&quot;}" data-module-id="PDP-RT-Office-Template|FAQTab|coreui-region|coreui-space-48pxaqz|coreui-space"> 
       <div class="m-small-space"> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-0alltiy" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;CollapsibleDrawer 4&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-collapsibledrawer&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m13r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:13,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r6a2&quot;}" data-module-id="PDP-RT-Office-Template|FAQTab|coreui-region|coreui-collapsibledrawer-0alltiy|coreui-collapsibledrawer"> 
       <section class="cui-drawer"> 
        <div class="cui-header f-divider"> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn1m13r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m13r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-0alltiy-collapsible-drawer0">How do I manage my Microsoft 365 subscription?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-0alltiy-collapsible-drawer0" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>To manage your billing information, install or remove Microsoft 365 or Office apps from additional PCs or Macs, and manage your installations of Office apps on other devices at any time, visit <a class="c-hyperlink" href="https://support.office.com/article/4414eaaf-0478-48be-9c42-23adc4716658">Install </a>&amp; <a class="c-hyperlink" href="https://support.office.com/article/Accounts-in-office-628ea040-f265-49de-b986-be09c3ebf8a9">Account management</a>.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn2m13r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:2,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m13r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-0alltiy-collapsible-drawer1">When does my subscription start?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-0alltiy-collapsible-drawer1" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>If you purchased a recurring billing subscription, your subscription starts when you complete your purchase.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>Recurring billing subscriptions may be purchased from Microsoft Store, the iTunes Store, the Mac App Store, and some other retailers. If you purchased a pre-paid subscription, your subscription starts when you activate your subscription on <a class="c-hyperlink" href="https://setup.office.com">https://setup.office.com/</a>. Pre-paid subscriptions may be purchased from a retailer or reseller, or a Microsoft support agent.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn3m13r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:3,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m13r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-0alltiy-collapsible-drawer2">How much OneDrive storage do I get with Microsoft 365?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-0alltiy-collapsible-drawer2" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>OneDrive is an online storage service that you can use to store documents, notes, photos, music, videos, or other types of files. With OneDrive you can access your files from nearly any device, and you can share them with others. <a class="c-hyperlink" href="http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=403718">Sign up for OneDrive</a>. The amount of additional storage that you get depends on your subscription:<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>Customers with an active Microsoft 365 Personal subscription receive an additional 1 TB of OneDrive storage per subscription plus 5 GB of storage for free.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>Customers with an active Microsoft 365 Family subscription receive an additional 1 TB of OneDrive storage per user, for up to 6 users, plus 5 GB of storage for one user. Each additional user must have their own Microsoft account and be added to the <a class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=831178">Microsoft Account site</a>.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>The additional storage is applied to the OneDrive account that is linked to the Microsoft account used to create the Microsoft 365 subscription. For Microsoft 365 Family, the storage is tied to the Microsoft accounts of the household members who have been added to the subscription.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn4m13r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:4,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m13r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-0alltiy-collapsible-drawer3">Which Microsoft account should I sign in with when using OneDrive?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-0alltiy-collapsible-drawer3" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>To access documents stored on OneDrive, sign into Microsoft 365 with the Microsoft account that you used to set up Microsoft 365. If you have <a href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=403719" class="c-hyperlink">shared your Microsoft 365 subscription</a> with other members of your household, they should sign in with their Microsoft account. <a href="http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=403720" class="c-hyperlink">Learn more about signing into Microsoft 365</a>. You can also sign into OneDrive directly at OneDrive.com.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn5m13r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:5,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m13r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-0alltiy-collapsible-drawer4">Are my documents stored in OneDrive also available offline?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-0alltiy-collapsible-drawer4" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>Yes. If youre using Windows 8.1 or Windows 10, OneDrive is preinstalled. To access your documents when youre not connected to the Internet, open File Explorer on your PC and go to the OneDrive folder. When you reconnect, OneDrive updates the online versions with changes you made offline.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>Visit the <a class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=808163">OneDrive for Windows 8.1</a> and <a class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=717896">OneDrive for Windows 10</a> support pages for more details.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>You can also download and install OneDrive on <a class="c-hyperlink" href="http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=403721">Windows 7, Windows Vista</a>, or on your <a class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=808164">Mac</a>. The OneDrive app creates a folder that automatically syncs between OneDrive and your computer, so you can work on your documentseven when youre offline.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn6m13r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:6,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m13r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-0alltiy-collapsible-drawer5">Why cant I have both a Microsoft 365 Family subscription and a Microsoft 365 Personal subscription?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-0alltiy-collapsible-drawer5" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>Your Microsoft account can have only one active Microsoft 365 consumer subscription. You can either convert your Microsoft 365 Family subscription to Microsoft 365 Personal, or you can wait until your current subscription expires before purchasing your Microsoft 365 Personal subscription.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn7m13r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:7,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m13r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-0alltiy-collapsible-drawer6">Are there other support options?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-0alltiy-collapsible-drawer6" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>For help and how-to content, visit <a href="https://support.microsoft.com" class="c-hyperlink">support.microsoft.com</a>. For free video-based training, visit&nbsp;<a class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=506713">www.office.com/training</a>.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </section> 
      </div> 
      <div id="coreui-areaheading-nf1fizl" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;AreaHeading 5&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-areaheading&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m14r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:14,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r6a2&quot;}" data-module-id="PDP-RT-Office-Template|FAQTab|coreui-region|coreui-areaheading-nf1fizl|coreui-areaheading"> 
       <div class="m-area-heading"> 
        <h2 class="c-heading">Renewals, cancellations, and billing</h2> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div id="coreui-space-dgy31nh" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;Space 5&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-Space&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m15r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:15,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r6a2&quot;}" data-module-id="PDP-RT-Office-Template|FAQTab|coreui-region|coreui-space-dgy31nh|coreui-space"> 
       <div class="m-small-space"> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-pw1zssi" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;CollapsibleDrawer 5&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-collapsibledrawer&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m16r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:16,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r6a2&quot;}" data-module-id="PDP-RT-Office-Template|FAQTab|coreui-region|coreui-collapsibledrawer-pw1zssi|coreui-collapsibledrawer"> 
       <section class="cui-drawer"> 
        <div class="cui-header f-divider"> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn1m16r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m16r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-pw1zssi-collapsible-drawer0">What billing options do I have for my Microsoft 365 subscription?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-pw1zssi-collapsible-drawer0" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>Recurring billing is the simplest way to ensure continued service. You can set up monthly or annual recurring billing by visiting <a class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=831178">the Microsoft Account site</a>.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>If you have a monthly subscription you can save money by converting it to an annual subscription at the&nbsp;<a class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=831178">Microsoft Account site</a>.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn2m16r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:2,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m16r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-pw1zssi-collapsible-drawer1">What happens when my subscription ends? How can I continue to work with my documents?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-pw1zssi-collapsible-drawer1" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>As the expiration date approaches, you will receive notifications in the Office apps and via email, alerting you to the upcoming expiration. If you choose to let your subscription expire, the Office apps enter read-only mode, which means that you can view or print documents, but you cant create new documents or edit existing documents.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>In read-only mode, you can still access and download your files for up to three months by signing into OneDrive directly using the Microsoft account you used to set up Microsoft 365. However, the additional storage that comes with your subscription is lost, so you must save your files elsewhere or buy more OneDrive storage if your OneDrive account exceeds the free storage quota of 5 GB.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>Note: If you need to create or edit Office documents, you can use online versions of Word, Excel, PowerPoint, and OneNote for free at <a class="c-hyperlink" href="https://office.com/">Office.com</a>. If you're using a Windows 10 device, you may already have the free Office Mobile apps installed. To learn more, see <a class="c-hyperlink" href="https://support.office.com/article/office-mobile-apps-for-windows-10-getting-started-d390fb3a-5d9a-4fa1-b798-a491c27fdfe9">Office Mobile apps for Windows 10: Getting started</a>.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn3m16r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:3,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m16r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-pw1zssi-collapsible-drawer2">I stopped sharing the subscription with a family member. What happens to the documents they stored in OneDrive?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-pw1zssi-collapsible-drawer2" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>They can still access and download their files by signing into OneDrive directly using their Microsoft account. If their OneDrive account exceeds the free storage quota of 5 GB, they'll need to save files elsewhere or buy more OneDrive storage.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn4m16r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:4,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m16r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-pw1zssi-collapsible-drawer3">Will I be notified before Im charged?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-pw1zssi-collapsible-drawer3" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>You will be notified before youre charged to continue your subscription for another year if you have an annual subscription. If you are signed up for a monthly subscription, your payment will be debited each month and you wont be notified in advance. You can change your payment method or cancel your subscription to stop future charges at any time by visiting <a href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=831178" class="c-hyperlink">your account</a> and signing in with the Microsoft account that you used to buy Microsoft 365.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn5m16r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:5,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m16r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-pw1zssi-collapsible-drawer4">How do I continue my Microsoft 365 subscription?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-pw1zssi-collapsible-drawer4" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>You have a few options to continue your subscription. Regardless of the option you choose, be sure to use the same Microsoft account that you used when setting up your subscription.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>If you have a recurring billing subscription, it will continue until cancelled. Your billing settings are shown on the <a class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=831178">Microsoft Account site</a> after you sign in with the Microsoft account that you used to buy Microsoft 365.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>If recurring billing is not enabled, visit <a class="c-hyperlink" href="http://www.microsoft365.com/renew">www.microsoft365.com/renew</a> to purchase a Microsoft 365 recurring billing subscription. The additional time will be automatically added to the remaining time on your existing subscription.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn6m16r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:6,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m16r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-pw1zssi-collapsible-drawer5">Will I keep my remaining subscription time if I pay early?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-pw1zssi-collapsible-drawer5" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>Yes. When you pay early to the same Microsoft 365 plan that you already have, the additional time is added to your existing subscription. For example, if you have two months left on your current subscription to Microsoft 365 Family and you pay for a one year subscription (12 months), your subscription will run for 14 more months.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn7m16r6a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:7,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m16r6a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-pw1zssi-collapsible-drawer6">How do I cancel my Microsoft 365 recurring billing subscription?</button> 
         <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-pw1zssi-collapsible-drawer6" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
          <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
          <p>If you purchased a recurring billing subscription from Microsoft via Microsoft Store or microsoft365.com, you have two options for cancelling:<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>You can cancel online by visiting the <a class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=831178">Microsoft Account site</a>, signing in with the Microsoft account that you used to buy your subscription, and then turning off recurring billing. With this approach, your subscription will automatically expire when your remaining subscription time is up.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>To cancel immediately, contact Microsoft support and request an immediate cancellation.<br> &nbsp;</p> 
          <p>If you purchased a recurring billing subscription from another retailer, you may have to cancel your subscription with that retailer. You can confirm this by visiting the <a class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=831178">Microsoft Account site</a>.</p> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </section> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </section>

    <div id="LivePersonVariation" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;LivePersonVariation&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_onestore-BuyboxVariationsContainer&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m1r1a3&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r1a3&quot;}" data-module-id="PDP-RT-Office-Template|footerRegion|coreui-region|LivePersonVariation|OneStore-BuyboxVariationsContainer">

  <script>
            if (window.addEventListener) {
                window.addEventListener("load", createSilentAuthFrame, false);
            } else if (window.attachEvent) {
                window.attachEvent("onload", createSilentAuthFrame);
            } else {
                window.onload = createSilentAuthFrame;
            }

            function InvokeSSOFrame(src) {
                var i = document.createElement("iframe");
                i.src = src;
                i.setAttribute("width", "0");
                i.setAttribute("height", "0");
                i.setAttribute("border", "0");
                i.setAttribute("frameborder", "0");
                i.setAttribute("style", "display: none");
                i.style = "display: none";
                document.body.appendChild(i);
            }

            function RefreshRemoteSSOSession(isUserAuthenticatedApi, silentPassport) {
                require(['jqReady!'], function ($) {
                    $.ajax(isUserAuthenticatedApi, {
                        type: "GET",
                        contentType: "text/plain",
                        xhrFields: {
                            withCredentials: true
                        },
                        crossDomain: true,
                        success: function (data) {
                            if (data.Status !== "Authenticated") {
                                InvokeSSOFrame(silentPassport);
                            }
                        }
                    });
                });
            }

            function createSilentAuthFrame() {
                var SSOCookieName = "ONERFSSO";
                if (document.cookie.indexOf(SSOCookieName) === -1) {
                    if ("False" === "True" && 1 !== 0) {
                            RefreshRemoteSSOSession("https://account.xbox.com/en-us/mscomhp/onerf/IsUserAuthenticated", "https://account.xbox.com/en-us/mscomhp/onerf/MeSilentPassport");
                    }
                    else {
                        InvokeSSOFrame("https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/microsoft-365/onerf/MeSilentPassport");
                    }
                    document.cookie = SSOCookieName + "=1";
                }
            }

        </script>
